Anyway, I called my own mobile phone to contact throughout the whole process. The door of the villa seemed to have some problems. It couldn‚Äôt be opened when the room card was fine. Later, the room service told me that I had to press hard. It is said that the hotel has only been open for two years, and the maintenance of this facility is a bit poor. When the hot spring is open, the water is cold, and the hot water will be used first. This point was not notified in advance. As a result, I was drenched in cold water and reported it for repair. Of course, although I complained a lot, it didn't affect my mood for playing, hahahaha.

Children are more interested in unpowered amusement rides, saving their parents' money.

Hygiene: Very good, no flaws found.
